# Paper + Live Trading Engine — Full Correctness Audit

**Date:** 2026-06-28  
**Branch:** feat/security-hardening  
**Method:** 16 specialist auditors over the live code (NOT the changelog) across math / execution / close / restart / bootup / freeze-recovery / concurrency / live-exchange, each finding adversarially verified by a code-truth reader + a reachability/impact skeptic, plus a completeness critic that spawned 6 follow-up audits. 215 agents, ~12.7M tokens.

## Tally

- **Confirmed: 85** — critical 2, high 19, medium 37, low 27
- **Needs human review: 5** (verifiers split)
- **Refuted: 6** (both verifiers refuted — listed at the end; one critical funding-sign claim among them flagged for independent re-check)

A finding is **confirmed** only when BOTH adversarial verifiers agreed; a split vote lands in **needs-review** (nothing dropped silently).

## Remediation status

Decision (operator, 2026-06-28): fix all four phases; canonicalize `pnl_pct` on the **equity-fraction** convention.

### Phase 1 — kernel-path safety parity ✅ (go-live blockers)
Root cause: the execution-kernel path is the DEFAULT for paper (`paper_kernel_execution=True`) and live (`live_kernel_execution=True`) but skipped the legacy path's safety machinery. Fixed + tested (`tests/test_engine_audit_phase1.py` + `tests/test_paper_control.py`; 195-test regression set green):

- **RISK-1** — kernel paper open now gated by `can_open(execution_type="paper", enforce_risk_caps=False)` in the dispatch loop (STOP / kill-switch / daily-halt / cooldown). Backfill opens bypass the gate so recorded history stays faithful. `scanner.py manage_positions_via_kernel`.
- **DIRECTION-BOOKS-1 / LIVE-4** — `_kernel_open_live_trade` routes via `books.resolve_open_book` (long-only skip + alert), sizes off the routed sub-account balance (fail closed if unreadable), runs the M7 cross-book guard, threads `book` into `_open_trade_db`/`register`/`can_open`. Books-off unchanged.
- **LIVE-1 / DIRECTION-BOOKS-2** — `_kernel_open_live_trade` wraps `_execute_direct`; a failed open goes to `_report_execution_failure` (self-heals the phantom OPEN, frees the slot, alerts).
- **LIVE-2** — `_kernel_close_live_trade` wraps `_execute_direct`, reports a failed close, holds OPEN for retry.
- **DB-4 / RACE-2** — `_kernel_close_live_trade` holds `pending_close_reconcile` rows (no reduce-only re-fire each scan).
- **DATA-2 / LIVE-5 / FREEZE-2** — `manage_positions_via_kernel` applies a last-closed-bar staleness gate: blocks NEW entries on stale candles, still manages existing positions.
- **HL-1** — `market_order` requires only the ENTRY leg; a filled entry whose protective leg was rejected is kept + surfaced via `protective_leg_failed`; `_execute_direct` arms the missing stop or flags `protective_stop_unarmed` + CRITICAL alert.
- **HL-3 / MANUAL-3** — `place_protective_stop` / `place_take_profit` fail CLOSED (return `error`) when no order id comes back.
- **RISK-3** — manual LIVE open requires a protective stop and re-asserts `is_trading_allowed()` at execution time.
- **RACE-1** — `run_scan` single-flights its execution phase (`_RUN_SCAN_EXEC_LOCK`); a concurrent in-process trigger degrades to signal-only.

### Phase 2 — promotion-gate integrity 🔶 (critical fix done; remainder pending)
Convention decision refined (operator, 2026-06-28): the literal "every close writes equity-fraction net_pnl_pct" re-breaks the H6 funding margin-scale contract (the previously-reverted path), so we use the **reader-side parity filter** instead.

- **PROMOTION-GATE-PARITY-2 (CRITICAL) + PARITY-3** ✅ — the kernel faithful paper close now stamps `pnl_is_equity_fraction=true` **atomically** with its net-pnl override (`scanner.py _kernel_close_recorded`, via `json_set`), and all four paper→live gate readers (`policy.py` — `_check_paper_trades`, `_check_paper_return`, `_check_paper_drawdown`, the S00152 gate; `_PARITY_PNL_FILTER`) now count ONLY equity-fraction parity rows. The gate can no longer compound mixed-unit pnl or promote on margin-scale legacy/converge/non-parity fills. H6 untouched. Tests: `tests/test_paper_gate_s00152.py::test_gate_excludes_non_equity_fraction_rows` + updated gate helper; 68-test gate/paper regression green. **Requires a paper re-baseline (reset + re-open kernel-managed) — on a non-rebased book the gate fails closed (no promotion), the safe direction.**
- **DB-1 / SCANAPPLY-2** ✅ — the kernel close is now ATOMIC: `close_trade_record` gained a `pnl_override` so status=CLOSED + pnl/pnl_pct/net_pnl_pct/pnl_usd + closed_at + the equity-fraction flag are written in ONE transaction (the separate override UPDATE that a crash could tear is gone). Non-override callers (legacy/manual) are byte-unchanged. Tests: `tests/test_engine_audit_phase2.py` (2). H6/double-count/reconcile/direction-book suites green (109).
- **Deferred Phase 2 tail (rationale):**
  - **PNL-2** (legacy/manual `pnl_usd` gross→net) — MEDIUM, low impact under kernel-default (non-kernel paper closes are rare); overwriting the established gross `pnl_usd` collides with the double-count contract. Bundle with the equity/sizing cleanup + re-baseline.
  - **PARITY-5** (live records margin-scale vs paper equity-fraction dashboard) — MEDIUM display-scale; recording an equity-fraction on the LIVE close reopens the H6 margin-scale tension on the live path — needs the same dedicated convention design.
  - **PARITY-1** (validation runs regime_gate=True via WFA, execution runs regime_gate=False) + **PARITY-4** (dead `compute_dual_score` regime-sensitivity detector) — **operator decision**: either run WFA ungated (match execution) or gate execution (match validation); both re-baseline the population. Coupled; flagged for a regime-parity decision, not changed unilaterally.

### Phase 3 — safety-control & live-orphan robustness 🔶 (in progress)
- **DAEMON-EQUITY-FEED-RISK-STATE-1** ✅ — in a LIVE session a transient paper-source equity fallback is now IGNORED (gated on `get_execution_mode()`), so the recovery tick can't re-baseline the HWM or clear a fired daily-loss halt; and a live↔live source-basis change no longer clears an already-fired halt. `risk.py update_equity`.
- **DAEMON-EQUITY-FEED-RISK-STATE-2** ✅ — the HWM (+ daily-loss denominator) now re-baselines on ANY real-source basis change (`books_aggregate`↔`exchange`), not just paper→non-paper, so disabling books can't compute a phantom ~100% drawdown that false-fires the kill-switch and force-flattens live positions. Tests: `tests/test_risk_module.py` (3 new); 55 risk + 133 reconcile/recovery green.
- **LIVE-EXCHANGE-RECONCILE-1** ✅ — the periodic (non-adopt) reconcile pass now places/repairs an EMERGENCY protective stop on any exchange position with no matching SQLite trade, so an orphan can't ride to liquidation naked until the next restart. `risk.py reconcile_exchange_positions`.
- **FREEZE-1** ✅ — new `health_monitor.check_scanner_execution`: goes RED when execution is active (open positions / execution enabled) but the EXECUTION scan is stale beyond the scanner job's cadence, so a hung position-manager (exits/stops not firing) is no longer invisible behind a green dashboard.
- **FREEZE-3** ✅ — new `health_monitor.check_daemon_liveness`: an alive-but-FROZEN daemon (process alive, market tick stale beyond `daemon_tick_max_stale_seconds`, default 600s) now goes RED, so a wedged daemon whose liquidation monitor + reconcile have silently stopped is detected. Both registered in the poll loop (so the critical-banner/Discord alert fires). Tests: `tests/test_engine_audit_phase3.py` (7); 111 health/runtime tests green.
- **RESTART-1 / RESTART-2** ✅ — `fetch_candles` no longer serves a short cache tail for a larger request: the shared cache holds `_CANDLE_CACHE_BARS` (360) rows but the kernel replay asks for `_paper_kernel_history_bars` (1500), and returning `cached_df.tail(1500)` truncated the replay so a position held past ~160 bars scrolled out of the window and lost ALL kernel exit enforcement (a zombie that could ride past its stop/time-stop), and downtime older than the cache dropped trades. Now the cache is served only when it COVERS the request; otherwise it direct-fetches the full window and republishes a covering cache (strict no-fallback mode serves the short cache but logs the truncation). The configured 1500-bar window is now actually delivered. Tests: `tests/test_engine_audit_phase3.py` (2). 77 scanner/paper tests green.
- **LIVE-EXCHANGE-RECONCILE-6** ✅ — a successful-but-EMPTY positions read (valid JSON, no exception) no longer mass-ghost-closes every tracked live position. `reconcile_exchange_positions` now requires N CONSECUTIVE empty-while-holding reads (`reconcile_empty_read_confirm_count`, default 2) before ghost-closing: a single glitch skips with `fetch_unavailable` and retries; a genuine simultaneous flatten (sustained empty) still reconciles. `risk.py`.
- **BOOT-1** ✅ — the API startup now stamps the startup-recovery gate `checking` (`daemon.mark_boot_recovery_pending`) BEFORE the scheduler/scanner thread spawns, so a stale `recovery_active=False` from a cleanly-exited prior run can't let a live entry through during the boot window before the daemon's boot reconcile verifies the exchange. A daemon-spawn failure releases the gate (`clear_boot_recovery_pending`) so paper isn't wedged. `api.py` lifespan + `daemon.py`. Tests: `tests/test_engine_audit_phase3.py` (RECONCILE-6 + BOOT-1, 3); 179 risk/reconcile/daemon/trading tests green.
- **Pending Phase 3 (mediums):** RECONCILE-2/3/4 (fill attribution by oid/hash; ghost-close funding/fee completeness). Auto-recovery wiring for the two new RED freeze checks is a follow-up (the alert fires today). DATA-6 (daemon cache window) follow-up would remove the per-scan re-fetch the RESTART-1 fix can trigger.

### Additional HIGH-severity fixes (a self-recheck caught five HIGHs missed by the first milestone claim)
- **LATE-1** ✅ — `_resolve_paper_go_live` now fails CLOSED on a reset-anchor read error (clamps the cutoff to now) instead of dropping the reset anchor and replaying pre-reset history into a freshly-emptied book. `scanner.py`.
- **MANUAL-1** ✅ — a manually PAUSED kernel position is now truly detached: the reconcile close/refresh appliers (paper + live) skip `manual_pause` rows, so pause-then-partial-close can't double-count PnL (paper) or re-close a detached live position. `scanner.py`.
- **MANUAL-2** ✅ — `_kernel_refresh_paper_trade` no longer clobbers an operator-set SL/TP (`stop_loss_source`/`take_profit_source == 'manual'`); the manual level is enforced, not reverted on the next scan. `scanner.py`.
- **DATA-1 + DATA-3** ✅ — `market_data.INTERVAL_TO_MS` now covers the HL-native interval set (30m/2h/3m/8h/12h/3d/1w were silently un-tradeable in live/paper), and `scanner._TIMEFRAME_SECONDS` covers the full canonical table so closed-bar trim + the stale-feed gate never silently use a 1h width for a 2h bar (partial-bar trading). 6h/45m remain non-HL-native (promotion-time timeframe validation is the follow-up).
- **DIRECTION-BOOKS-3** ✅ — `_trade_routed_address` reads books settings via the re-raising `kv_get` and returns an UNRESOLVABLE sentinel on a locked-DB read, so the reconcile scope EXCLUDES a routed sub-account trade rather than mis-scoping it into the master ghost-close pass and auto-closing a real position. `risk.py`.
- Tests: `tests/test_engine_audit_phase3.py` (DATA/LATE/MANUAL/DIRECTION-BOOKS-3) + the existing manual/scanner/direction-book suites. 183 green.

**Milestone:** both CRITICALs + every HIGH-severity finding across Phases 1–3 are now fixed and tested (19/19 highs + PNL-1's gate impact). Remaining work is MEDIUM/LOW robustness + cleanup + the population re-baseline.

### Phase 4 — pending
Parity/cleanup (KERNEL/KCOPY/RECON edges, DATA-1/3/6 timeframe coverage, the many lows) + the population re-baseline. Per-finding detail below.

## CONFIRMED — CRITICAL (2)

### `DIRECTION-BOOKS-ACCOUNTING-1` — Kernel-live OPEN path (default ON) bypasses ALL direction-book routing: no resolve_open_book, no long-only short-skip, no per-book sizing, no cross-book/min-notional guards, book stamped NULL

- **Severity:** CRITICAL  |  **Mission:** direction-books-accounting  |  **Confidence:** high
- **Location:** `forven/scanner.py:5836-5882 (_kernel_open_live_trade), 6040-6042 + 6093 + 6619-6623 (dispatch), 5828 (_live_kernel_execution_enabled default True); contrast legacy forven/scanner.py:4324-4371,4377-4390,4587-4604,4413,4720-4726`
- **Claim:** With the default live_kernel_execution=True, a vectorizable live strategy is executed by manage_positions_via_kernel(execution_type='live') -> _kernel_open_live_trade, which never consults forven/exchange/books.py at all. So a books-ENABLED live deployment is systematically mis-routed: every position opens on the master wallet (book=NULL), shorts are placed even in long-only mode (the short-skip is silently dropped), the per-book equity read and the cross-book self-trade guard and the min-notional preflight never run, and sizing reads the wrong wallet.
- **Impact:** Direction-book isolation is completely defeated on the default live path. (a) Long-only fail-OPEN: with books enabled and no short sub-account, shorts the operator believes are impossible are placed for real on the master wallet. (b) Mis-sizing: sizing_equity for the live kernel path is `_get_real_account_equity()` (scanner.py:6041), which the daemon sets to the books-AGGREGATE equity (daemon.py:1166 source 'books_aggregate' -> state['account_equity'] at daemon.py:1461-1462), i.e. the SUM across master+long+short, yet the order is placed only on master, so the position is sized off total capital but margined against a fraction of it (oversize -> margin rejection/strand, or wrong size either way). (c) A long-strat and a short-strat that books exist to let coexist are both forced onto master where can_open Rule 2 one-per-asset blocks the second (missed trades / divergence from backtest). The only way to get correct book routing today is to ALSO set live_kernel_execution=False, which sacrifices backtest parity; the operator cannot have both.
- **Suggested fix:** In _kernel_open_live_trade, before opening, call books.resolve_open_book(direction): on a skip reason, surface long-only and return without opening; otherwise resolve the book, read the routed sub-account equity (books-enabled) for sizing instead of the aggregate, run the cross-book and min-notional guards, and pass book=open_book into both _open_trade_db and register so _execute_direct routes the order (and the eventual close) to the correct sub-account. Alternatively, hard-block enabling live_books_enabled while live_kernel_execution is True (mutual exclusion) until the kernel path is books-aware.
- **Evidence:** _kernel_open_live_trade calls `trade_id = _open_trade_db(strat_id, asset, direction, ref_price, units, risk_pct, float(leverage), signal_data, execution_type="live")` (scanner.py:5873) with NO book= kwarg, then `_execute_direct("open", ...)` (5880). _open_trade_db defaults `book: str | None = None` (scanner.py:3790) so book is stored NULL. can_open is called without book= (5855: `can_open(asset, direction, strat_id, execution_type="live", enforce_risk_caps=False)`). A grep for `books.|resolve_open_book|book_address|open_book` in scanner.py returns matches ONLY in the legacy path (4290-4720) and helpers, none inside 5690-6179. The legacy path, by contrast, does `open_book, book_skip_reason = books.resolve_open_book(direction)` (4329), the long-only skip `if open_book is None: ... actions.append(f"SKIPPED {strat['asset']} short — long-only")` (4356-4371), the per-book equity read with fail-closed (4331-4354), the cross-book guard `_opposite_book_would_cross` (4377-4390), the min-notional preflight (4587-4604), and stamps `_open_extra = {"book": open_book}` into _open_trade_db (4720-4726). live_kernel_execution=`_scanner_bool_setting("live_kernel_execution", True)` (5828); no code forces it OFF when live_books_enabled is ON (api_core.py:2490-2497 only blocks DISABLING books while routed trades are open).
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): The code literally does what the claim states. Default live_kernel_execution=True (scanner.py:5828). For a vectorizable LIVE-stage strategy, dispatch routes to manage_positions_via_kernel(execution_type="live") at scanner.py:6619-6623 (this elif precedes the legacy fall-through, which is only reached when the kernel returns None i.e. non-vectorizable, 6677-6710; _is_live_kernel_stage @5831-5833, _is_kernel_paper_strategy paper-only @5315-5319). The open applier _kernel_open_live_trade (5836-5882) never imports/calls books — a scanner.py-wide grep for books.|resolve_open_book|book_address|open_book|books_enabled hits ONLY helpers (450-481, 3578-3613) and the legacy path (4290-4720), nothing in 5690-6179. It calls _open_trade_db(...execution_type="live") at 5873 with NO book= kwarg; the param defaults book=None (3790) so book is stored NULL, and calls can_open(...execution_type="live") at 5855 with NO book=. _execute_direct routes via _resolve_trade_vault_address(strict=True) (3277), which reads SELECT book FROM trades (3594) and returns None for NULL book (3596-3597) => master wallet. So every kernel-live position opens on master.

Legacy contrast verified exactly as cited: resolve_open_book (4329), long-only short-skip returning pre-open (4356-4371), per-book equity fail-closed (4331-4354), cross-book guard (4377-4390), min-notional preflight (4587-4604), book=open_book stamped into _open_trade_db (4720-4726).

Impacts confirmed: (a) can_open (risk.py:490-716) has NO long-only/short-book guard — only resolve_open_book enforces it — so a short in long-only mode places a REAL short on master (fail-OPEN). (b) Live sizing reads _get_real_account_equity() (6041) -> daemon_state["account_equity"] (scanner.py:534-538), which the daemon sets to the books-AGGREGATE (daemon.py:1165-1170 source 'books_aggregate' -> 1461-1462) when books are on; the order is placed only on master => mis-sized. (c) can_open's live scope with book=None filters to master-routed positions (risk.py:646-652), so a long-strat and short-strat both stamped NULL collide in the master pool and Rule 2 (673-681) blocks the second — defeating the coexistence books exist to provide. api_core.py:2486-2508 only blocks DISABLING live_books_enabled while routed trades are open; there is no mutual exclusion with live_kernel_execution, and live_kernel_execution is not handled there at all.

Sole precondition (acknowledged in the finding): the operator must enable live_books_enabled (default False, books.py:62-64). It is a real, supported, operator-facing feature. Given the bug is a fail-OPEN (real shorts placed when the operator believes shorts are impossible) plus mis-sized real-money orders and broken position accounting, critical is appropriate when books are enabled; severity unchanged.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: high): All technical claims verified against live code. (1) live_kernel_execution defaults True (scanner.py:5828). (2) _kernel_open_live_trade (scanner.py:5836-5882) never consults forven/exchange/books.py; a grep of books|resolve_open_book|book_address|open_book|book= across scanner.py shows matches ONLY in helpers and the legacy path (425-481, 1041, 3564-3613, 4290-4720) and ZERO inside the kernel path 5690-6179. (3) can_open is called without book= (5855); risk.py:646-652 then scopes the live position pool to _routed_addr(None)=master, and Rule 2 one-per-asset (risk.py:672-681) blocks a second strategy on the same asset — so a long+short pair that books exist to isolate collide on master (claim c). (4) _open_trade_db is called without book= (5873) and defaults book=None (3790), inserted verbatim (3821-3825), so book is stored NULL. (5) The legacy path does full routing: resolve_open_book (4329), per-book fail-closed equity (4330-4354), long-only short-skip (4356-4371), cross-book guard (4377-4390), min-notional preflight (4587-4604), and stamps book=open_book into can_open (4413) and _open_trade_db (4720-4726). (6) Sizing uses sizing_equity=_get_real_account_equity() (6041), which reads daemon_state.account_equity (scanner.py:533-538) written from risk_snapshot.equity (daemon.py:1461-1462) derived from _book_aware_account_value -> source 'books_aggregate' summing master+sub-accounts (daemon.py:1077-1171), while the order routes only to master — confirming the oversize/mis-margin claim (b). (7) No code forces live_kernel_execution OFF when books are on; api_core.py:2486-2508 only refuses to DISABLE books while routed trades are open. The long-only fail-OPEN (claim a) is real: with the short-skip dropped, shorts the operator believes impossible are placed on the master wallet. REACHABILITY: the defect requires live_books_enabled=True, which defaults False (books.py:64), and real impact requires mainnet (FORVEN_ALLOW_MAINNET=1; testnet otherwise per scanner.py:5824). Direction books is a deliberate, fully-built, infrastructure-backed operator feature, not dead code, and once enabled the default kernel live path silently defeats its entire purpose with no guard — so the bug is genuine and reachable, but only after the operator opts into a non-default feature. Per the reachability lens (a real bug behind a default-off flag warrants reduced severity), I downgrade critical to high: severe money/state impact when triggered, but not a silent loss on the DEFAULT configuration.

### `PROMOTION-GATE-PARITY-2` — ->live paper gate compounds mixed-scale pnl (equity-fraction kernel rows + leverage-margin legacy rows) into total_return/drawdown/Sharpe/PF — corrupts the real-money promotion decision

- **Severity:** CRITICAL  |  **Mission:** promotion-gate-parity  |  **Confidence:** high
- **Location:** `forven/policy.py:3713-3724 and 3892-3915 (compute_live_metrics); forven/policy.py:1244,1275 (readiness UI); forven/scanner.py:5509,5544-5550 vs trade_state.py:268 and scanner.py:3722-3723`
- **Claim:** The live-promotion gate aggregates `COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct)` over all paper trades and compounds them as `equity *= (1.0 + pnl)`. But that column carries two incompatible units: kernel paper closes write an EQUITY-FRACTION (gross*size_fraction, e.g. ~0.01-0.03 for 1%-risk sizing), while legacy/manual/converge/late closes write a LEVERAGE-INCLUSIVE MARGIN-RETURN (price_move*leverage, no size_fraction, e.g. 0.10-0.30+). They differ by roughly 1/size_fraction. Compounding them together produces a fabricated equity curve, total_return, max_drawdown, profit_factor and Sharpe.
- **Impact:** The real-money ->live decision is made on garbage aggregates: a single mis-scaled legacy/margin win (e.g. +0.30) can inflate total_return and PF and FALSE-ACCEPT a strategy; a single margin loss (the MEMORY 'fake -95%' cross-asset splice → equity*=0.05) tanks total_return/max_dd and FALSE-REJECTS a winner. The same distortion is shown to the operator in check_paper_live_readiness (policy.py:1244,1275).
- **Suggested fix:** Normalize the column to ONE convention before it ever reaches the gate (preferred: persist kernel-style equity-fraction net for every close path), OR have the gate read a single canonical equity-impact field and reject/segregate rows lacking it. Do not COALESCE across two unit systems. At minimum compute the gate metrics only over rows that carry the kernel equity-fraction.
- **Evidence:** Gate query + aggregation: policy.py:3713-3724 `SELECT COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct) AS pnl_pct FROM trades ... LIKE 'paper%' ... ; pnls = [...]; live = compute_live_metrics(pnls)`. Compounding: policy.py:3895-3896 `equity *= max(0.0, 1.0 + pnl)`. Kernel = equity-fraction: scanner.py:5509 `pnl_pct_net = float(trade.get("pnl_pct") or 0.0)  # kernel net, equity-fraction` and 5544-5545 `UPDATE trades SET pnl_pct=?, net_pnl_pct=?, ... (round(pnl_pct_net,8), round(pnl_pct_net,8), ...)`; execution_kernel.py:14 `pnl_pct = (price_return*sign*leverage - drag) * size_fraction` and :114 `pnl_pct = gross * size_fraction`. Legacy = margin-return: trade_state.py:268 `pnl_pct = ((resolved_exit_price - entry_price) / entry_price) * signed * leverage` (NO size_fraction), and scanner.py:3722-3723 writes `net_pnl_pct = float(gross_pnl_pct) - fees_pct` on that same leverage-inclusive scale.
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Every cited line checks out against the live code. The ->live promotion gate (policy.py:3713-3724) and the readiness UI checks (policy.py:1244-1252, 1275-1283) all run `SELECT COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct) ... WHERE ... execution_type LIKE 'paper%'` over ALL paper rows (no kernel_managed/source filter) and feed compute_live_metrics, which compounds `equity *= max(0.0, 1.0+pnl)` (policy.py:3896) for total_return/max_drawdown and computes profit_factor/sharpe over the same raw list (policy.py:3882-3906). No normalization sits between the trades column and the gate.

The column genuinely carries two incompatible units: (a) the kernel faithful close writes an EQUITY-FRACTION into both pnl_pct and net_pnl_pct — scanner.py:5509 `pnl_pct_net = float(trade.get("pnl_pct"))  # kernel net, equity-fraction` and 5544-5545/5549-5550 `UPDATE trades SET pnl_pct=?, net_pnl_pct=? (round(pnl_pct_net,8),...)`, with the kernel formula `pnl_pct = gross * size_fraction` (execution_kernel.py:114, size_fraction=margin/equity → true equity impact); (b) the legacy/manual/converge/late paths write a LEVERAGE-INCLUSIVE MARGIN-RETURN with no size_fraction — trade_state.py:268 `pnl_pct = ((resolved_exit_price-entry_price)/entry_price)*signed*leverage`, surfaced by close_trade_record and netted at scanner.py:3722-3723 `fees_pct = 2.0*(fee_bps/10000)*leverage; net_pnl_pct = float(gross_pnl_pct)-fees_pct`. These scales differ by ~1/size_fraction (size_fraction<<1 for risk-based sizing → 10-100x).

Both writers are reachable for paper rows: manual close (scanner.py:5714, explicitly "for paper positions," and it skips kernel_managed rows at 5701) writes margin-return; the gated paper-only late hop-in deliberately does NOT override pnl_pct/net_pnl_pct (scanner.py:5524-5537), leaving close_trade_record's margin-return; the converge/forced close (scanner.py:5912) writes margin-return. The MEMORY-documented S04545 "fake -95%" cross-asset splice is a concrete production instance of a margin-return row landing among kernel rows. The `equity *= (1+pnl)` compounding is only valid for the kernel equity-fraction convention, so any mix (or even an all-margin-return strategy) corrupts total_return/max_dd/PF/Sharpe.

This is the real-money ->live decision basis, and a single mis-scaled row can false-accept a losing strategy into live trading or false-reject a winner; severity critical is appropriate (it is the direct gate on deploying real money). The only refutation would require 100% of paper closes to flow through the kernel faithful path, which is false given the reachable manual/late/converge writers. Confirmed.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: high): The code-level defect is REAL and verified. Kernel paper closes persist an EQUITY-FRACTION net to both pnl_pct and net_pnl_pct (execution_kernel.py:114 `pnl_pct = gross * size_fraction`; written at scanner.py:5544-5545 `round(pnl_pct_net,8), round(pnl_pct_net,8)`), while close_trade_record/manual/converge closes persist a LEVERAGE-INCLUSIVE MARGIN return with NO size_fraction (trade_state.py:268 `pnl_pct = ((resolved_exit_price - entry_price)/entry_price)*signed*leverage`; scanner.py:3722-3723 derives net on the same margin scale; manual exits at scanner.py:5714 do the same). The promotion gate (policy.py:3713-3724) and the operator readiness checks (_check_paper_return policy.py:1244, _check_paper_drawdown policy.py:1275) both `SELECT COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct) ... LIKE 'paper%'` with NO kernel/parity filter and compound via `equity *= max(0.0, 1.0 + pnl)` (policy.py:3896). The two units differ by ~1/size_fraction, so any margin-scale row mixed with equity-fraction rows fabricates total_return/max_drawdown (and, for genuinely mixed series, PF/Sharpe too). REACHABILITY is confirmed under default-on flags but NOT via the mechanisms the finding headlines: late hop-in is HARD-DISABLED (scanner.py:6069 `late_entry_enabled = False`, explicitly "Hard-off (not operator-gateable)"), and the cited 'fake -95%' cross-asset splice now closes FLAT at entry → pnl 0 (scanner.py:5675-5679), so that catastrophic example cannot occur. The live mixing sources are: converge-orphan closes (scanner.py:5646, gated paper_kernel_converge_orphans default True), manual exits on a kernel strategy (scanner.py:5714 → _close_trade_db), and wholly-margin-scale non-vectorizable strategies on the default-on legacy fallback (_paper_legacy_fallback_enabled default True, scanner.py:6630-6660; these are flagged 'must not be promoted on these numbers' but the gate enforces no such block). The common case — a pure kernel-managed auto-promoted strategy — is internally consistent equity-fraction and is evaluated CORRECTLY. Because the defect corrupts a promotion guard / operator display (mis-routing real money under non-common conditions) rather than silently losing money on the common path, and the catastrophic example is neutralized, and PF/Sharpe are scale-invariant for single-convention legacy strategies (finding slightly overstates), I downgrade critical → high. The fix recommendation (normalize to one convention, or restrict the gate to rows carrying the kernel equity-fraction net) is sound; the gate query genuinely lacks any convention guard.

## CONFIRMED — HIGH (19)

### `PNL-1` — net_pnl_pct/pnl_pct scale blend: kernel writes an EQUITY-fraction, legacy/manual/converge write a MARGIN-return, and the paper promotion gate compounds them together

- **Severity:** HIGH  |  **Mission:** pnl  |  **Confidence:** high
- **Location:** `forven/policy.py:1244,1275,3714 (gate reads); forven/scanner.py:5509-5552 (kernel close, equity-fraction); forven/trade_state.py:268 + forven/scanner.py:3706-3745 (legacy/manual close, margin-return)`
- **Claim:** The deferred net_pnl_pct scale-blend is still live. Kernel-closed paper trades store pnl_pct = net_pnl_pct = an EQUITY-fraction (gross*size_fraction, net of drag+funding). Legacy/manual/converge closes store a MARGIN-return (price_return*leverage, NOT size-scaled). All three promotion-gate readers select COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct) over execution_type LIKE 'paper%' and compound them in compute_live_metrics, mis-scaling any book that mixes paths.
- **Impact:** Worked example (entry 100, exit 110, long, lev 3, size_fraction 0.3, fee 4.5bps/slip 2bps): kernel net_pnl_pct = (0.10*3 - 0.0039)*0.3 = 0.0888 (8.88% of equity); legacy net_pnl_pct = 0.30 - 0.0027 = 0.2973 (29.7%). Same trade, ~3.3x apart. Short (entry 100, exit 90) is sign-correct on both but the same 3.3x scale gap. A legacy-path or mixed paper book is compounded as if margin-returns were equity-returns, overstating total_return_pct by roughly 1/size_fraction. Because the live gate (policy.py:3735) requires total_return > min_total_return_pct, an under-performing strategy whose true equity return is below the floor can clear the inflated floor and be deployed with real money.
- **Suggested fix:** Make ONE convention: have close_trade_record (and _close_trade_db) write the size-scaled EQUITY-fraction (multiply the margin-return by the recorded size_fraction), OR have the gate read a single canonical equity-return column. At minimum, exclude trades flagged non-parity / closed via close_price_source in {kernel_converge, cross_asset_cleanup, manual_close} or persist the parity flag so the gate can filter, instead of blending scales.
- **Evidence:** Kernel: scanner.py:5509 `pnl_pct_net = float(trade.get("pnl_pct") or 0.0)  # kernel net, equity-fraction`; finalize() in execution_kernel.py:111-114 `gross = ((exit-entry)/entry)*sign*leverage - round_trip_drag` then `pnl_pct = gross * size_fraction`; written to BOTH columns at scanner.py:5544-5545 `UPDATE trades SET pnl_pct=?, net_pnl_pct=? ... (round(pnl_pct_net,8), round(pnl_pct_net,8), ...)`. Legacy/manual: trade_state.py:268 `pnl_pct = ((resolved_exit_price - entry_price) / entry_price) * signed * leverage` (no size_fraction), then scanner.py:3723 `net_pnl_pct = float(gross_pnl_pct) - fees_pct`. Converge/cross-asset (scanner.py:5646-5650, 5675-5679) call close_trade_record only -> net_pnl_pct stays NULL, COALESCE falls back to the margin-return pnl_pct. Gate: policy.py:1244 `SELECT COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct) AS pnl_pct ... LIKE 'paper%'` and compute_live_metrics (policy.py:3895-3896) `equity *= max(0.0, 1.0 + pnl)` compounds each value as an equity-fraction. Reachable: non-vectorizable paper strategies run the legacy engine BY DEFAULT (scanner.py:6704 manage_positions; gate _paper_legacy_fallback_enabled default True at scanner.py:5239) and their non-parity status is only stamped into an in-memory diagnostics dict (scanner.py:6657-6663), never excluded by the gate.
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Every link in the chain holds against the live code. (1) KERNEL writes an EQUITY-fraction: execution_kernel.py:114 `pnl_pct = gross * size_fraction` (gross = price_return*leverage - drag, line 111); scanner.py:5509 reads it (`# kernel net, equity-fraction`) and 5544-5545 writes the SAME value to BOTH pnl_pct AND net_pnl_pct. (2) LEGACY/MANUAL writes a MARGIN-return: trade_state.py:268 `pnl_pct = ((exit-entry)/entry)*signed*leverage` (no size_fraction; close_trade_record's UPDATE at 284-307 never touches net_pnl_pct), and the legacy engine manage_positions (def 3840) computes the same at scanner.py:4104 and routes to _close_trade_db, which sets net_pnl_pct = gross_pnl_pct - fees_pct (scanner.py:3722-3723) — still margin-scaled. (3) CONVERGE orphan: _kernel_close_orphan (scanner.py:5646-5650) calls close_trade_record only (no _close_trade_db), so net_pnl_pct stays NULL and COALESCE falls back to the margin-return pnl_pct. (The cross-asset orphan at 5675-5679 closes FLAT at entry, PnL~0, so it is scale-invariant — the finding over-includes it, but this does not weaken the core defect.) (4) GATE blends scales: policy.py:1244, 1275, 3714 all `SELECT COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct) ... LIKE 'paper%'`, and compute_live_metrics compounds each value as an equity return `equity *= 1.0 + pnl` (policy.py:3896), feeding the live deploy floor at 3735. A grep of policy.py for vectoriz/parity/close_price_source/kernel_converge/cross_asset returned NO matches, confirming the gate cannot exclude non-parity legacy or converge trades. (5) REACHABLE: _paper_legacy_fallback_enabled default True (scanner.py:5239); scanner.py:6652-6704 trades non-vectorizable PAPER strategies on the legacy engine and only stamps non-parity into the in-memory diagnostics_out dict (6657-6663); sizing.py:228-240 + default_controls (255-269) show size_fraction is well below 1.0 for the default atr profile and all risk-based modes (only sizing_mode=full gives 1.0), so the two conventions genuinely diverge. The fail direction is fail-OPEN: margin-returns overstate the equity return by ~1/size_fraction, inflating total_return_pct so an under-floor strategy can clear the live-deploy return gate with real money. Worked example matches (~3.3x at size_fraction 0.3). Severity high is appropriate: not a silent in-flight money loss (which would be critical) but a wrong gate metric that fails open toward deploying an underperforming strategy with real capital; it is conditional on the legacy/converge path being active, which is default-enabled and also reachable on kernel strategies via data-source-switch converge closes.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): VERIFIED against live code at every cited file:line. (1) Kernel paper close writes a size-scaled EQUITY-fraction: execution_kernel.py:111-114 computes gross = price_return*leverage - drag then pnl_pct = gross*size_fraction; scanner.py:5509 labels it 'kernel net, equity-fraction' and writes it to BOTH pnl_pct and net_pnl_pct at scanner.py:5544-5545/5549-5550. (2) Legacy/manual closes write a MARGIN-return with NO size_fraction: trade_state.py:268 pnl_pct = price_return*signed*leverage; _close_trade_db (scanner.py:3676) recomputes net_pnl_pct = gross_pnl_pct - fees_pct at scanner.py:3723; legacy manage_positions feeds the same margin-return at scanner.py:4104/4140 and manual exits at scanner.py:5714-5717. (3) Converge close (scanner.py:5646-5650) calls close_trade_record only, leaving net_pnl_pct NULL so COALESCE falls back to the margin-return pnl_pct; cross-asset close (5675-5679) exits at entry => pnl_pct 0 (harmless, finding mildly over-lists it). (4) All three gate readers COALESCE(net_pnl_pct, pnl_pct) over execution_type LIKE 'paper%' (policy.py:1244,1275,3714) and compute_live_metrics compounds each as an equity-fraction equity *= max(0,1+pnl) (policy.py:3896), driving the real-money live floor min_total_return_pct (policy.py:3735). REACHABILITY confirmed: legacy fallback default ON (_paper_legacy_fallback_enabled -> _scanner_bool_setting('paper_legacy_fallback_enabled', True), scanner.py:5239) routes non-vectorizable paper strategies to manage_positions (scanner.py:6704), producing a pure-margin book inflated ~1/size_fraction; the non-parity flag lives only in the in-memory diagnostics_out dict (scanner.py:6657-6663) and a grep of policy.py for vectoriz/parity/runtime_type/close_price_source/size_fraction and execution_decision/non_parity returned NO matches, so the gate cannot exclude these trades. No normalization pass reconciles the two scales (exchange/risk.py:2270-2276 live recovery also writes a margin-return net). The 1/size_fraction scale gap and the 'underperformer clears an inflated live floor -> real money' impact are correct. Severity stays high (not critical: it mis-scales a promotion-gate metric rather than directly mis-filling or silently losing money on a live order, but it yields wrong numbers users act on and can gate real-money deployment incorrectly).

### `LATE-1` — kv_get fail-open in _resolve_paper_go_live silently drops the reset anchor → a freshly-reset paper book replays pre-reset history (persistent corruption)

- **Severity:** HIGH  |  **Mission:** late  |  **Confidence:** high
- **Location:** `forven/scanner.py:5302-5312 (with scripts/reset_paper_trades.py:85-94 and forven/db.py:3516-3519)`
- **Claim:** The whole defense against replaying pre-reset trades into an emptied book is the global reset KV. _resolve_paper_go_live reads it inside `try: reset_raw = kv_get(...) except Exception: reset_raw = None`. A transient kv_get failure (SQLite 'database is locked' is RE-RAISED by kv_get, not swallowed) makes reset_raw None, which is INDISTINGUISHABLE from 'never reset' — so go-live falls back to the still-old `stage_changed_at`. For a strategy that was in paper before the reset, that cutoff predates the reset, and since the reset deleted all its trades, the next scan backfills every reproducible pre-reset trade back into the fresh book.
- **Impact:** A single transient DB-lock during one strategy's per-scan kv_get reintroduces the exact pre-reset-replay the reset script was written to prevent. The wrongly-backfilled trades persist (the reconciler never deletes, and _kernel_trade_exists then blocks their removal), permanently corrupting the paper equity curve — which feeds sizing and promotion decisions.
- **Suggested fix:** Fail CLOSED on a kv_get error: distinguish read-failure from genuine absence. On exception, either skip recording this scan or clamp the cutoff to a conservative value (e.g. get_now() or the bounded default 6-bar window) instead of falling back to the older stage_changed_at. Optionally have the reset also stamp each affected strategy's stage_changed_at so the per-strategy anchor alone is safe.
- **Evidence:** scanner.py:5302 `try: reset_raw = kv_get(PAPER_BOOK_RESET_KV_KEY, None)` / 5304 `except Exception: reset_raw = None` / 5306 `candidates = [ts for ts in (_parse_iso_ts(strat.get('stage_changed_at')), _parse_iso_ts(reset_raw)) if ts is not None]` / 5310 `if not candidates: return None` / 5312 `return min(max(candidates), get_now())`. db.py:3516-3519 kv_get: `except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc: if 'no such table: kv'...: return default; raise` (locks are re-raised). reset_paper_trades.py:85-90 comment: 'Without it [the KV stamp], a still-old stage_changed_at would make the next scan replay the whole pre-reset history into the fresh book'; the script stamps ONLY the global KV (line 94) and never bumps per-strategy stage_changed_at.
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): The code literally exhibits the claimed fail-open defect, and every cited line is accurate. scanner.py:5302-5305 wraps the kv_get read in `try/except Exception: reset_raw = None`. db.py:3516-3519 shows kv_get re-raises sqlite3.OperationalError unless the message is "no such table: kv" — so a "database is locked" error is genuinely re-raised and caught by the broad except, collapsing reset_raw to None. With reset_raw=None, scanner.py:5306-5312 builds candidates from stage_changed_at only and returns min(max([stage_changed_at]), now) = the old pre-reset stage_changed_at, which is indistinguishable from the genuine never-reset case. scanner.py:6054-6055 then sets recent_cutoff to that pre-reset timestamp.

The corrupting consequence verifies against paper_reconcile.py:158-160: a kernel-finalized closed trade with no recorded counterpart and entry_time >= recent_cutoff is backfilled. After reset_paper_trades.py wipes the trades (lines 97-104) the recorded set is empty, so every reproducible pre-reset trade (entry >= old stage_changed_at) is re-recorded into the fresh book on that one bad scan. The corruption is permanent: the reconciler has no delete path; on a later scan where kv_get succeeds and recent_cutoff becomes the reset stamp, those backfilled closed rows (now entry < cutoff) just hit `matched.add(id(r))` at paper_reconcile.py:165 — never removed. The reset script (reset_paper_trades.py:91-94) stamps ONLY the global KV and never bumps per-strategy stage_changed_at, confirming the global KV is the sole defense.

Caveat on reachability/severity framing: get_db() (db.py:434,444) sets timeout=60 and PRAGMA busy_timeout=60000, so a truly *transient* lock on a WAL-mode SELECT is absorbed for 60s before raising — the claim's "single transient DB-lock" overstates likelihood; it needs a sustained (>60s) lock or another exception type, plus a prior reset to have occurred (an infrequent operator action). kv_set stores json.dumps (db.py:3544) so the value round-trips cleanly and json.loads won't throw normally, narrowing the realistic trigger. Despite the rare trigger conjunction, this is a genuine fail-open where fail-closed is required, with permanent, silent corruption of the paper equity curve that feeds sizing and promotion-to-live decisions. Keeping severity at high: the persistent corruption and its influence on live-deployment decisions justify it even though the trigger is a low-probability edge case.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: medium): Code logic fully verified. scanner.py:5302-5305 `_resolve_paper_go_live` catches ALL exceptions from kv_get and sets reset_raw=None, which is indistinguishable from 'never reset'; candidates (5306-5309) then collapse to stage_changed_at and the cutoff (5312) reverts to the pre-reset anchor — a genuine fail-open. db.py:3516-3519 confirms kv_get swallows only 'no such table: kv' and re-raises lock OperationalErrors. reset_paper_trades.py:91-94 stamps only the global KV, never per-strategy stage_changed_at, so the per-strategy anchor alone is unsafe. paper_reconcile.py:159 & 197 gate backfill/open solely on recent_cutoff; with the cutoff reverted to old stage_changed_at, _recent() is True for every pre-reset entry in df, so they backfill into the emptied book (scanner.py:6144-6145). Backfill is bounded only by df (window_start guards orphan_close only), and nothing deletes the injected rows — subsequent good scans match them as no-ops (paper_reconcile.py:165), so corruption persists and feeds the equity curve/sizing/promotion. So the defect and its corruption path are real and reachable.\n\nSeverity downgraded from high to medium on reachability: db.py:434,444 sets WAL mode + busy_timeout=60000 on every connection, and kv_get is a pure SELECT. Under WAL, readers do not block on writers and essentially never raise SQLITE_BUSY from write contention; a read raising OperationalError requires a >60s lock — a pathological event, not the routine 'transient DB-lock' the finding's framing implies. The bug also requires the narrow window right after a manual reset_paper_trades.py --apply (which advises pausing the scanner first), is paper-only (_is_kernel_paper_strategy), and its money impact is indirect (corrupted paper equity → promotion), not a direct loss. Real fail-open worth fixing (fail closed: clamp cutoff to get_now()/bounded window on read failure, or have reset also bump per-strategy stage_changed_at), but low trigger probability and paper-scoped/indirect impact put it at medium, not high.

### `LIVE-1` — Live kernel OPEN does not handle _execute_direct failure: phantom OPEN trade + held risk slot + no operator alert, later booked as a fabricated CLOSED PnL

- **Severity:** HIGH  |  **Mission:** live  |  **Confidence:** high
- **Location:** `forven/scanner.py:5872-5882 (caller loop 6142-6143, 6154-6155); compare legacy forven/scanner.py:4024-4032`
- **Claim:** On the gated live path, _kernel_open_live_trade inserts the OPEN trade row and reserves a risk slot BEFORE calling _execute_direct, but does NOT wrap _execute_direct in try/except and never calls _report_execution_failure. If the real order placement raises (market_order error, set_leverage failure, inverted-stop refusal, halt re-assert, or missing-order-id RuntimeError), the exception propagates to the action loop which only log.error()s it. The legacy _open_via_execution catches the same failure and calls _report_execution_failure(action='open') -> _fail_unfilled_open_trade(), which marks the phantom FAILED (no PnL), releases the slot, and emits a trade_failed notification.
- **Impact:** A failed live open leaves a phantom OPEN trade that holds a risk slot indefinitely (re-added on every _rebuild_portfolio_positions) and, via the unique-open index, BLOCKS all future opens for that (strategy,asset,direction) until the delayed stale-cleanup fires. No operator notification or developer handoff occurs. When _cleanup_stale_unfilled_open_trades eventually runs (only on a status/API read, after the 180s grace), it routes the phantom through close_trade_record, which — because _open_trade_db already set entry_price=ref_price (modeled) — computes a FABRICATED pnl from the modeled entry and a cached price and records it as a CLOSED live trade, corrupting the strategy's live track record (vs. the legacy path's clean FAILED, no PnL).
- **Suggested fix:** Wrap _execute_direct in _kernel_open_live_trade (and the close in _kernel_close_live_trade) in try/except and call _report_execution_failure(action='open'|'close', trade_id, reason) on failure, mirroring the legacy _open_via_execution/_close_via_execution, so the phantom is cleaned to FAILED (no PnL), the slot released, and the operator alerted.
- **Evidence:** _kernel_open_live_trade: `trade_id = _open_trade_db(...execution_type="live")` (5873) then `register(...)` (5877) then unguarded `_execute_direct("open", trade_id, strat_id, asset, direction, units, ref_price, stop_loss=stop_price, take_profit=target_price, leverage=float(leverage))` (5880-5881). Caller: `except Exception as exc: log.error("[%s] kernel %s %s action failed: %s", ...)` (6154-6155) — no failure routing. Legacy contrast: `except Exception as e: ... _report_execution_failure(strategy_id=strat_id, action="open", trade_id=trade_id, reason=str(e))` (4024-4031).
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Verified end-to-end against live code. (1) scanner.py:5872-5882 — _kernel_open_live_trade guards _open_trade_db only for sqlite3.IntegrityError (5874) and register() with try/except-pass (5876-5879), then calls _execute_direct("open",...) at 5880-5881 with NO try/except and never invokes _report_execution_failure. (2) Caller: scanner.py:6142-6143 invokes open_applier; the only handler is 6154-6155 `except Exception as exc: log.error(...)` — no failure routing. (3) Reachability confirmed: scanner.py:6093 `open_applier = _kernel_open_live_trade if is_live else _kernel_open_paper_trade`, with is_live True for live-stage strategies (6027) and live_kernel_execution default ON. (4) _execute_direct genuinely raises on the open path — scanner.py:3337 (ValueError no-stop), 3345 (RuntimeError halt re-assert), 3354-3356 (RuntimeError set_leverage failure), 3373 (RuntimeError market_order error) — exactly the listed modes; the legacy path wraps the same call in try/except (4010-4032), corroborating that it raises. (5) Legacy contrast confirmed: scanner.py:4024-4032 catches and calls _report_execution_failure(action="open",...), which routes to _fail_unfilled_open_trade (3130) marking the phantom FAILED not CLOSED (3176), releasing the slot (3186), and emits a trade_failed operator notification (3196/3220). (6) Fabricated-CLOSED-PnL impact verified: _open_trade_db inserts entry_price=signal_entry_price=ref_price (modeled) with fill_entry_price NULL (3819-3828); the phantom is NOT skipped by _cleanup_stale_unfilled_open_trades (trading.py:537-543 — fill_entry NULL, no pending_open_reconcile, not local-only paper since execution_type='live'), which routes via _close_stale_open_trades to close_trade_record where entry_price falls back from NULL fill_entry_price to the modeled entry_price (trade_state.py:245-249) and, with a cached exit_price, computes non-null pnl_pct/pnl_usd and sets status='CLOSED' (267-274, 287). This is precisely the fabricated outcome _fail_unfilled_open_trade's docstring (3138) exists to prevent. The close-side gap noted in the suggested fix is also real (_execute_direct at 5900 is unguarded), though close failures are intentionally not converted to FAILED. Severity 'high' is appropriate: it does not directly drain real funds (the order failed, no real fill), but it silently corrupts the live track record with a fabricated CLOSED PnL, holds/blocks a risk slot for that (strategy,asset,direction) until delayed cleanup, and suppresses the operator alert that the legacy path emits — wrong numbers users act on plus a real recoverable failure.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Verified against live code. (1) forven/scanner.py:5872-5882: _kernel_open_live_trade does _open_trade_db(execution_type="live") at 5873 and register() at 5877, then calls _execute_direct("open",...) at 5880-5881 with NO try/except. (2) _execute_direct("open") genuinely raises before any fill is recorded: ValueError no-stop (3337), RuntimeError halt (3345), RuntimeError set_leverage failure (3354-3356), RuntimeError market_order error (3373) — so fill_entry_price stays NULL. (3) The only handler is the per-action loop at scanner.py:6131-6155, which catches with `log.error(...)` at 6154-6155 and never calls _report_execution_failure; the exception is swallowed inside the loop, so no outer handler routes it. (4) Legacy contrast confirmed at 4010-4032 (try/except -> _report_execution_failure(action="open", trade_id, reason)). A grep shows ALL _report_execution_failure call sites (1212/3928/3955/4003/4026/4163) are legacy; the kernel open/close path has none. (5) _open_trade_db (3786-3837) inserts entry_price=ref_price (modeled) + signal_entry_price, status OPEN, never fill_entry_price; the unique-open index idx_trades_unique_open (3831) blocks future opens and the register() slot is never released. (6) _fail_unfilled_open_trade (3130-3193) — the clean FAILED/no-PnL/release path — is reached only via _report_execution_failure, so it is skipped. (7) Fabricated PnL impact confirmed: _cleanup_stale_unfilled_open_trades (trading.py:509-558) skips only fill_entry>0 (537-539) and local-only paper (531); the live NULL-fill phantom qualifies after the 180s grace, calling _close_stale_open_trades (366-444) -> close_trade_record (trade_state.py:245-307), which falls back to modeled entry_price (245-249) and computes pnl from (cached exit - modeled entry) (267-274), writing status='CLOSED' (284-307); if no cached price it closes "incomplete" but still CLOSED, never FAILED. No trade_failed notification fires from this path. Reachability: live_kernel_execution defaults True (5828) — this is the default live path for live/live_graduated/deployed stages; real-money impact is gated behind FORVEN_ALLOW_MAINNET=1 (testnet by default), but the state corruption (held slot, blocked reopens, corrupted track record, no alert) is real regardless and the failure modes are realistic in production. Severity HIGH is appropriate: it does not leave an unhedged REAL position (raises are pre-fill; a post-fill DB raise leaves a correctly-OPEN managed position skipped by the >0-fill guard), but it corrupts the live track record with a fabricated CLOSED PnL users act on, silently holds/blocks a risk slot, and suppresses the operator alert.

### `LIVE-4` — Kernel live path bypasses direction-book routing and the long-only short-skip (opens all auto live trades on the master wallet)

- **Severity:** HIGH  |  **Mission:** live  |  **Confidence:** medium
- **Location:** `forven/scanner.py:5855 (can_open w/o book), 5873 (_open_trade_db w/o book), 3595-3597 (NULL book -> master); legacy 4329,4356-4368,4413; books.resolve_open_book books.py:124-149`
- **Claim:** _kernel_open_live_trade calls can_open(...) and _open_trade_db(...) WITHOUT a `book` argument, so the trade's book column is NULL and _resolve_trade_vault_address returns None = master wallet. It never calls books.resolve_open_book, so when direction books (Approach C) are enabled it (a) routes every kernel-auto live position to the master wallet instead of the long/short sub-account, and (b) bypasses the long-only-mode guard that the legacy path uses to SKIP shorts when no short sub-account is configured.
- **Impact:** With live_books_enabled=True (the documented Approach C / $100k-volume long-only scenario) and live_kernel_execution defaulting ON, a deployed strategy's SHORT signal opens a real SHORT on the MASTER wallet even though the operator is in long-only mode — directly violating the configured risk posture and the long-only protection. It also collapses long/short isolation (longs and shorts net on master) and bypasses the M7 cross-book self-trade guard. Gated behind the opt-in books feature (default off), so no impact when books are disabled.
- **Suggested fix:** In _kernel_open_live_trade, resolve the routing book via books.resolve_open_book(direction); honor the skip_reason (skip the short, surface the long-only warning), pass book to both can_open and _open_trade_db, and run the M7 _opposite_book_would_cross check — mirroring the legacy manage_positions path.
- **Evidence:** `allowed, alloc_risk, why = can_open(asset, direction, strat_id, execution_type="live", enforce_risk_caps=False)` (5855) — no book. `trade_id = _open_trade_db(strat_id, asset, direction, ref_price, units, risk_pct, float(leverage), signal_data, execution_type="live")` (5873) — no book, so column NULL. _resolve_trade_vault_address: `book = dict(row).get("book") ...; if not book: return None` (3595-3597) = master. Legacy contrast: `open_book, book_skip_reason = books.resolve_open_book(direction)` (4329); short-in-long-only skip `actions.append(f"SKIPPED {strat['asset']} short — long-only ...")` (4368); `book=open_book` passed to _open_trade_db (4413). resolve_open_book returns (None, 'LONG ONLY: short-book sub-account is not configured — short signal skipped...') for shorts when no short book (books.py:140-147).
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Verified the full chain against live code. Dispatch: _apply_execution_actions (scanner.py:6619-6623) routes live-stage strategies through manage_positions_via_kernel(execution_type="live") whenever _live_kernel_execution_enabled() (default ON, 5828) and _is_live_kernel_stage; no books check. The kernel open applier is _kernel_open_live_trade (6093, is_live branch). In _kernel_open_live_trade (5836-5882): can_open(...) is called WITHOUT book (5855), and _open_trade_db(...) is called WITHOUT book (5873). _open_trade_db's signature defaults book=None (3790) and inserts it into the trades.book column (3821-3826), so the column is NULL. _execute_direct (3277) routes via vault_address = _resolve_trade_vault_address(trade_id, strict=True); for a NULL book the function returns None (3595-3597) = master wallet. The kernel path never calls books.resolve_open_book, so it neither honors the long-only short-skip nor the M7 _opposite_book_would_cross guard. Confirmed by grep: the only books_enabled/live_books references in scanner.py are in the legacy manage_positions path (4324-4587); manage_positions_via_kernel has none. Legacy contrast confirmed: resolve_open_book(direction) (4329), long-only skip + early return (4356-4371), M7 cross-book guard (4377-4390), book=open_book to can_open (4413), and _open_extra={"book": open_book} to _open_trade_db (4720/4726). books.resolve_open_book (books.py:124-149) returns (None, "LONG ONLY...") for shorts with no short book. books_enabled defaults False (books.py:64), so the defect only manifests when the operator enables live_books_enabled (Approach C) — exactly as the finding scopes it. One minor imprecision: the evidence cites line 4413 as the legacy _open_trade_db book-pass, but 4413 is the can_open book arg; the legacy _open_trade_db book-pass is at 4720/4726. This does not affect the substance. Severity unchanged at high: gated behind an opt-in feature (off by default) but, when enabled, opens real shorts on the master wallet in long-only mode, collapses long/short isolation, and bypasses the self-trade guard — a genuine money/risk-posture defect the legacy path explicitly prevents.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Chain verified end-to-end against live code. (1) _kernel_open_live_trade calls can_open(asset, direction, strat_id, execution_type="live", enforce_risk_caps=False) (scanner.py:5855) and _open_trade_db(..., execution_type="live") (scanner.py:5873) with NO book argument; both signatures default book=None (risk.py:495; scanner.py:3790), so trades.book inserts NULL (scanner.py:3821-3825). (2) NULL book -> master wallet: _resolve_trade_vault_address does `book = dict(row).get("book"); if not book: return None` (scanner.py:3595-3597), and _execute_direct routes the REAL order via vault_address = _resolve_trade_vault_address(trade_id, strict=True) (scanner.py:3277), so None = master. (3) A grep for books./_opposite_book_would_cross shows ZERO book routing, long-only short-skip, or M7 cross-guard anywhere in the kernel live path (_kernel_open_live_trade 5836+, dispatcher 6027-6179); all such logic lives only in legacy manage_positions (4326-4390) and the close resolver. (4) Legacy contrast confirmed: resolve_open_book (4329), short-in-long-only skip `SKIPPED ... long-only` (4368), M7 cross guard (4377-4390), book=open_book to can_open (4413); resolve_open_book returns (None, 'LONG ONLY: ...') for shorts with no short sub-account (books.py:140-148). Reachability: dispatch at scanner.py:6619-6623 routes live-stage strategies through the kernel when _live_kernel_execution_enabled() (default True, 5828) with NO live_books_enabled check, and the legacy books path is only a non-vectorizable fallback (6630-6652), so normal vectorizable live strategies never reach the legacy book logic. Gating is correctly scoped: live_books_enabled defaults False (books.py:64); when OFF, resolve_open_book returns ('main', None) so legacy also routes to master and there is NO divergence/impact — exactly as the finding states. When an operator enables books (the documented Approach C / $100k-volume long-only mainnet scenario), the bug is real: a SHORT the legacy path would SKIP instead opens a REAL short on the master wallet (violating long-only posture), long/short isolation collapses, M7 self-trade guard is bypassed, and sizing uses master equity (_get_real_account_equity, 6041) instead of the book sub-account balance (legacy _book_account_equity, 4336). Severity high is well-calibrated: impact-when-triggered is severe real-money/state corruption, but it is gated behind a default-off opt-in feature (which the finding honestly acknowledges), so it does not affect the default deployment.

### `HL-1` — market_order/limit_order discard an already-FILLED entry and raise when a protective (SL/TP) leg is rejected, creating an unprotected orphan position

- **Severity:** HIGH  |  **Mission:** hl  |  **Confidence:** medium
- **Location:** `forven/exchange/hyperliquid.py:1280-1305 (_require_bulk_order_ids), 1401-1430 (market_order), 1538-1563 (limit_order); callers forven/api_domains/paper_control.py:586-624; forven/daemon.py:819-821 vs 1509-1514`
- **Claim:** bulk_orders submits [entry, stop, tp] as a NON-atomic batch. If the IOC entry fills (gets an oid/avgPx) but a protective leg is rejected per-status (e.g. trigger 'would immediately trigger' in a fast adverse move, or a tick/precision rejection on the cap leg), _require_bulk_order_ids sees the stop/tp label missing and — because a per-status rejection produces NO top-level result['error'] key — raises RuntimeError, discarding the entry fill (price, oid, filled_size). The function never returns the fact that a real position is now open.
- **Impact:** Scanner path (scanner.py:4010-4032): exception is caught, trade left OPEN with pending_open_reconcile; the position is UNPROTECTED until the next periodic reconcile re-arms it via risk.py _repair_position_protection (bounded but real exposure window in exactly the fast-market conditions where the stop matters most). Manual path (paper_control.py:591-592): market_order raises BEFORE _open_trade_db_safe runs, so the filled position is written to NO DB row; periodic reconcile does NOT adopt (daemon.py:1512 calls reconcile_all_books without adopt_missing_in_sqlite; only startup at 819-821 adopts), so the orphan stays untracked AND unprotected until the daemon is restarted. Real money at risk.
- **Suggested fix:** When the ENTRY leg returned a fill/oid, do NOT raise: return the entry fill payload AND a structured flag (e.g. protective_leg_failed + which leg) so the caller can record the position and immediately place the missing protective stop (or emergency-close). Reserve the hard raise for the case where the entry itself has no fill/oid. Also make periodic reconcile adopt orphans, or run an immediate exchange-verify after a failed multi-leg open.
- **Evidence:** _require_bulk_order_ids: `missing_labels = [label ... if str(label) not in order_ids]; if not missing_labels: return; error = str((result or {}).get('error') or '').strip(); if error: return; ... raise RuntimeError('Missing HyperLiquid order IDs for ' + ...)` (1287-1305). market_order calls it unconditionally after submit (1403-1408). A real HL per-order rejection is `{"status":"ok","response":{"data":{"statuses":[{"error":...}]}}}` — no top-level 'error', so the `if error: return` escape never fires and it raises even though statuses[0] for the entry filled.
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Verified against live code. (1) _require_bulk_order_ids (forven/exchange/hyperliquid.py:1287-1305) only escapes its raise via the TOP-LEVEL result['error'] key (1291-1293). A HyperLiquid per-order rejection returns overall status:"ok" with the error nested in response.data.statuses[i] (no top-level error), so the escape never fires and it raises. (2) _extract_bulk_order_ids (1233-1247) omits a rejected leg's label (an error status has no oid/resting/filled) but DOES extract the filled entry's label, so missing_labels=[the rejected protective leg] while the entry has filled. (3) market_order calls _require_bulk_order_ids at 1403-1408 and limit_order at 1541-1546, BOTH before the fill payload is constructed/returned (1409-1430 / 1547-1563) — so the already-FILLED entry (avgPx/totalSz/oid present in result) is discarded by the raise. Mechanism confirmed exactly as claimed. Caller impacts confirmed: MANUAL path (paper_control.py:586-592) converts the raise to HTTPException 502 at 591-592 BEFORE _open_trade_db_safe (620), so no DB row is written for the live filled position. SCANNER path (scanner.py:4010-4032, 4753-4846) catches the exception and keeps the pre-created trade row OPEN with pending_open_reconcile (4818-4825) — a bounded window. Daemon adoption asymmetry confirmed: startup reconcile sets adopt_missing_in_sqlite=True (daemon.py:819-821) but the periodic reconcile (daemon.py:1509-1514) passes only _get_testnet() positionally so adopt defaults to False (risk.py:2345). Critically, the periodic reconcile cannot even repair the manual orphan's protection: db_by_asset is built only from trades WHERE status='OPEN' (risk.py:1986); with no DB row the orphan asset is absent from db_by_asset, the exchange-position loop (2023) falls to `if adopt_missing_in_sqlite:` (2095) which is False, and the position is skipped with no _repair_position_protection and no discrepancy. Result: an untracked AND unprotected live position persisting until daemon restart. Only minor overstatement: an operator-triggered control-plane reconcile (ops.py:590, adopt=True) could also recover it without a restart, but the default automated loop will not. Severity 'high' is well-calibrated: the trigger requires a conditional per-leg exchange rejection (not deterministic), and the dominant automated scanner path is self-healing, while the manual-path untracked-orphan outcome edges toward critical but is gated on the manual live-open endpoint.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Verified end-to-end against live code. (1) hyperliquid.py:1287-1305 _require_bulk_order_ids raises RuntimeError when a protective label has no oid, gated only on `result.get("error")`; a per-status HL rejection lives in response.data.statuses[i].error (no top-level "error" key), and a grep of every "error" producer in the module (1334/1341/1364/1457/1465/1502/1609/1782-84) confirms the top-level key is only set by Forven's own pre-submit guards or close_position — never by a raw bulk_orders per-status rejection. _submit (140-179) returns the SDK response unchanged. So the `if error: return` escape never fires for this case and it raises. (2) _extract_bulk_order_ids (1222-1247) populates order_ids["entry"] from statuses[0].filled while the rejected stop/tp label is absent → missing_labels non-empty → raise. (3) market_order (1403-1408) and limit_order (1541-1546) invoke the helper BEFORE building/returning the payload (1410+/1547+), so the already-filled entry (oid/avgPx/size) is discarded. SCANNER path: _execute_direct (3369) lets the raise propagate (no in-function stop fallback); scanner.py:4024-4032 catches it, marks the trade pending_open_reconcile and keeps it OPEN (4815-4846). risk.py:2024-2094 shows a still-OPEN matched trade IS re-armed by even the periodic reconcile via _repair_position_protection — bounded unprotected window. MANUAL path: paper_control.py:586-592 raises → HTTPException(502) before _open_trade_db_safe (620), so NO DB row for the filled position. daemon.py:821 startup passes adopt_missing_in_sqlite=True, but the periodic reconcile (1509-1514) calls reconcile_all_books(_get_testnet()) positionally and the default is False (risk.py:2345); the unmatched-position branch only adopts/repairs when adopt is True (2095), otherwise it just appends a missing_in_sqlite discrepancy (2198-2201) with NO protection repair — so the manual orphan stays untracked AND unprotected until a daemon restart. The risk.py:783-794 comment explicitly names this exact failure mode, corroborating it is real and known. Reachability: LIVE-only (paper uses sim_market_order at 1321-1323), no default-off flag gating the order path; trigger is a per-status protective-leg rejection while the IOC entry fills (would-immediately-trigger in a fast adverse move, tick/precision/min-notional on the protective leg) — uncommon but concentrated in exactly the volatile conditions where the stop matters. Impact and sizing as stated are correct. Severity high is appropriate: a real, live-reachable unprotected-position window (scanner) escalating to a naked untracked orphan until restart (manual). The only residual uncertainty is the empirical frequency of the triggering HL rejection, but the defect itself is unambiguous in code, so I keep this confirmed rather than needs_human_review.

### `MANUAL-1` — manual_pause does NOT detach a kernel-managed position from the reconciler → pause+partial-close double-counts PnL (paper) / re-closes a 'detached' LIVE position

- **Severity:** HIGH  |  **Mission:** manual  |  **Confidence:** high
- **Location:** `forven/api_domains/paper_control.py:325-334, 405-421; forven/scanner.py:5368-5375, 5382, 5504-5552`
- **Claim:** The partial-close double-count guard requires the operator to PAUSE a kernel-managed position before partial-closing, on the stated premise that pausing 'detaches' it so the reconciler won't re-close the full original size. But manual_pause is NOT honored anywhere on the kernel reconcile path: a paused kernel trade is still fed to the reconciler and is later re-closed at its FULL original kernel PnL (size-independent), double-counting the partially-closed units. On LIVE it places a real reduce-only close on a position the operator explicitly detached.
- **Impact:** Paper equity/track-record is silently inflated (or deflated) by the partial slice's PnL whenever the documented pause-then-partial-close workflow is used on the DEFAULT (kernel) paper path. That corrupted paper performance feeds the promotion gate, so a strategy can be promoted to LIVE on fabricated numbers. On LIVE, a paused kernel position is still flattened by a real reduce-only order at the kernel's exit — a real-money action contradicting the operator's explicit detach.
- **Suggested fix:** Honor manual_pause on the kernel reconcile path: in _kernel_recorded_trades skip rows with manual_pause (so paused kernel trades are excluded from the snapshot), OR short-circuit close/refresh appliers when the recorded row's signal_data has manual_pause. Additionally, _kernel_close_recorded should scale PnL by the residual size when partial_closes exist, or partial-close should strip kernel_managed/kernel_entry_time from the residual so it is no longer reconciled.
- **Evidence:** Guard (paper_control.py:326): `if bool(_sd.get("kernel_managed")) and not bool(_sd.get("manual_pause")):` raise 409 telling the operator to 'Pause management for this strategy first, then partial-close.' Partial-close then only shrinks size + appends audit (paper_control.py:418-421): `UPDATE trades SET size = ?, signal_data = ? WHERE id = ?` (parent stays kernel_managed, retains kernel_entry_time, status OPEN). But _kernel_recorded_trades includes ANY trade with kernel_entry_time unconditionally (scanner.py:5368-5375 `kref = sd.get("kernel_entry_time")` then `out.append({... "status":"open" ...})`); the manual_pause skip (scanner.py:5382 `if sd.get("manual_pause") or ... "manual": continue`) is reached ONLY in the `elif is_open` ORPHAN branch (no kernel_entry_time). When the kernel finalizes that entry, reconcile emits a close (paper_reconcile.py:161-163) and _kernel_close_recorded books PnL from the FULL position ignoring the shrunken size (scanner.py:5510-5511 `equity_at_entry = sd.get("kernel_equity_at_entry")`, `pnl_usd = round(float(equity_at_entry) * pnl_pct_net, 4)`; written at 5544-5550). The child leg already booked its slice (paper_control.py:353 `pnl_usd = (fill - entry) * close_qty * signed`). Only the LEGACY engine honors pause (scanner.py:4037), and _kernel_handle_manual_exits skips paused (scanner.py:5701) — neither is the reconcile path.
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Every link in the chain holds against live code. (1) paper_control.py:326 blocks partial-closing a kernel-managed position unless manual_pause is set, with a 409 telling the operator to pause first on the premise that pausing detaches it. (2) set_manual_pause (paper_control.py:818-825) only writes manual_pause/manual_pause_set_at — it does NOT strip kernel_managed or kernel_entry_time. (3) Partial-close (paper_control.py:418-421) only shrinks size + appends a partial_closes audit; the parent stays OPEN, kernel_managed, with kernel_entry_time; the child leg books its slice at line 353 (fill-entry)*close_qty*signed. (4) _kernel_recorded_trades (scanner.py:5368-5375) appends ANY row carrying kernel_entry_time as open/closed unconditionally; the manual_pause skip at 5382 lives only inside the elif-orphan branch, which is unreachable when kernel_entry_time exists. (5) manage_positions_via_kernel (scanner.py:6076-6088) splits recorded trades only by asset and feeds same_asset_recorded straight into reconcile with no manual_pause filter. (6) reconcile (paper_reconcile.py:161-163) emits a close for the matched recorded OPEN once the kernel finalizes that entry. (7) _kernel_close_recorded (scanner.py:5510-5511, written 5544-5550) computes pnl_usd = kernel_equity_at_entry * pnl_pct_net — using the ORIGINAL full-position equity, untouched by partial-close, fully size-independent. (8) _get_paper_strategy_equity (scanner.py:604) is SUM(pnl_usd) over all CLOSED paper trades, so the child slice and the full-size parent both count → the slice's entry→kernel-exit PnL is double-booked, corrupting paper equity/track-record that feeds the promotion gate. (9) manual_pause is honored only on the legacy engine (scanner.py:4037-4042) and _kernel_handle_manual_exits (5701, manual non-kernel positions) — neither is the reconcile path. (10) On LIVE, _kernel_close_live_trade (scanner.py:5885-5928) places a real reduce-only order via _execute_direct at line 5900 with no manual_pause check, flattening a position the operator explicitly detached (the live close at 5896 uses the shrunken row size, so live has no PnL double-count, but the unwanted real close is confirmed). (11) The kernel path is the default for both paper and live (scanner.py:6614, 6619) and both functions are wired to API routes (routers/paper.py:119-120, :153). Severity left at high: wrong numbers users/promotion act on plus a real recoverable live action, but gated behind a specific operator workflow rather than firing automatically, so not critical.
  - _reachability_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Confirmed on the DEFAULT path. Flags paper_kernel_execution (scanner.py:5222) and live_kernel_execution (scanner.py:5828) both default True, so the kernel reconcile path is live for paper AND live. set_manual_pause (paper_control.py:818-825) only merges {"manual_pause":True} into signal_data; it does NOT strip kernel_managed/kernel_entry_time. partial_close (paper_control.py:418-421) shrinks size + appends partial_closes audit but leaves the parent OPEN with kernel_entry_time intact. _kernel_recorded_trades (scanner.py:5368-5375) appends EVERY trade with kernel_entry_time unconditionally; the manual_pause skip at scanner.py:5382 is only reachable in the elif-is_open ORPHAN branch (no kernel_entry_time), so it never fires for a paused kernel trade. manage_positions_via_kernel feeds that paused trade into reconcile (scanner.py:6076,6085); reconcile emits a close when the kernel finalizes the entry (paper_reconcile.py:161-163). PAPER: _kernel_close_recorded books pnl_usd = equity_at_entry * pnl_pct_net (scanner.py:5510-5511) = FULL position PnL ignoring the shrunken size, while the partial child already booked its slice (paper_control.py:353) → slice PnL double-counted, silently corrupting paper equity/track-record feeding the promotion gate. LIVE: _kernel_close_live_trade (scanner.py:5885-5913) places a REAL reduce-only order via _execute_direct (5900) with NO manual_pause check on a position the operator explicitly detached. The guard's premise (pause detaches it) is therefore false, and following the only permitted partial-close workflow corrupts state. One minor inaccuracy in the finding's evidence: the live applier computes dollar PnL on the residual size (5913), so live is not a dollar double-count like paper — but the finding's stated live impact (an unwanted real reduce-only order on a detached position) holds exactly. Severity high is correct: real, silent, and on the default path, but gated behind a manual operator workflow with bounded paper magnitude rather than an automatic per-trade loss.

### `MANUAL-2` — Manual SL/TP set on a kernel-managed PAPER position is overwritten/erased by the next reconcile refresh — accepted but never enforced

- **Severity:** HIGH  |  **Mission:** manual  |  **Confidence:** high
- **Location:** `forven/api_domains/paper_control.py:670-679, 712-725; forven/scanner.py:5617-5626; forven/strategies/paper_reconcile.py:170-178`
- **Claim:** adjust_stop_loss / adjust_take_profit place no guard against kernel-managed positions, so an operator can set a manual absolute SL/TP on a kernel position; it is written to signal_data and shown in the UI. But while the kernel still holds that position, every scan emits a 'refresh' that overwrites stop_loss_price/take_profit_price with the kernel's own levels (or None), so the operator's manual stop never holds — the position rides to the kernel's stop instead.
- **Impact:** An operator who tightens or sets a protective stop on a kernel-managed paper position sees it accepted and displayed, but it is reverted within one scan and never enforced — the exact 'manual SL accepted but never enforced' failure. The position then exits only at the kernel's (often wider) stop, a larger loss than the operator intended; paper results diverge from what the UI implies the operator controlled.
- **Suggested fix:** In _kernel_refresh_paper_trade, do not clobber operator-set levels: skip the refresh (or the SL/TP keys) when the recorded signal_data has stop_loss_source/take_profit_source == 'manual' (or manual_pause). Alternatively, guard adjust_stop_loss/adjust_take_profit against kernel-managed positions the way partial-close is guarded — but only after MANUAL-1's pause-detach is actually implemented.
- **Evidence:** adjust_stop_loss (paper_control.py:670-673) resolves the open trade and calls _adjust_protective with NO kernel_managed check; _adjust_protective writes `updates = {price_key: float(parsed), source_key: "manual", ...}` then `_update_open_trade_signal_data(trade_id, updates)` (paper_control.py:712, 725). Next scan, reconcile matches the still-open kernel position to the recorded row and emits a refresh (paper_reconcile.py:175-177), whose applier overwrites the levels unconditionally: scanner.py:5618-5621 `updates = {"stop_loss": pos.get("stop_price"), "stop_loss_price": pos.get("stop_price"), "take_profit": pos.get("target_price"), "take_profit_price": pos.get("target_price")}` then `_update_trade_signal_data(...)`. That merge does NOT drop None (scanner.py:3042 `signal_data.update(_clean_signal_data(updates))`; _clean_signal_data only unwraps numpy scalars, scanner.py:3777-3784), so a kernel with no stop ERASES the manual SL and a kernel with a stop REPLACES it. The refresh only skips late_entry (scanner.py:5615); there is no manual / stop_loss_source==manual / manual_pause skip.
  - _code-truth_ → **confirmed** (sev: unchanged): Code literally exhibits the defect, and the chain is even stronger than claimed.
